msg:I went to Xiamen for a trip during the May Day holiday. I spent a long time choosing this old five-star hotel. The hotel is not in the downtown area. The rooms are clean and soundproof. I can't hear people talking in the corridor. The waiters are well-trained and polite. There are fruits and snacks every day. Although the same fruits, apples and tangerines, are available every day, it is better than most hotels. It is not close to the subway, but there is a bus express station nearby. The bus express station is a dedicated road, so there is no need to worry about traffic jams. It is not far to take a taxi to popular scenic spots. The facilities are slightly lacking in that the light switch is not convenient to set. You have to go to the bedside to find the main switch. The toilet in the bathroom is very close to the bathroom door. The air conditioner switch is also an old-fashioned switch, but the air conditioning cooling effect is not affected, and the air conditioner does not make much noise, so the old-fashioned switch is harmless. The price did not increase too much during the May Day holiday. The price is similar to that of chain hotels near some popular scenic spots. Of course, it is a old-fashioned five-star hotel that makes people feel at ease, haha. Overall, it is satisfactory and cost-effective. I will consider staying again when I travel to Xiamen in the future.
